25:T3d84,<entryFree id="n11381" key="خَلْقٌ" type="main">     
                  <form>       
                     <itype>1</itype>        
                     <orth orig="" extent="full" lang="ar">خَلْقٌ</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">خلق</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">خلقة</orth>
                  </form> signifies The act of <hi rend="ital">measuring;</hi> or <hi rend="ital">determining the measure, proportion,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">the like,</hi> of a thing; and the <hi rend="ital">making</hi> a thing <hi rend="ital">by measure,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">according to the measure of another thing;</hi> or <hi rend="ital">proportioning</hi> a thing <hi rend="ital">to another thing;</hi> syn. <foreign lang="ar">تَقْدِيرٌ</foreign>: (S, Msb, K, TA, and Bd in ii. 19:) this is the primary meaning. (Msb, TA, and Bd ubi suprà.) You say, <foreign lang="ar">خَلَقَ الأَدِيمِ</foreign>, (S, Msb, K,) aor.      
    <form n="infl">       
                     <orth orig="Bu" lang="ar">خَلُقَ</orth>
                  </form>, (S, TA,) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">خَلْقٌ</foreign> (JK, S, Msb, K) and <foreign lang="ar">خَلْقَةٌ</foreign>, (K,) <hi rend="ital">He measured,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">proportioned,</hi> (<foreign lang="ar">قَدَّرَ</foreign>,) <hi rend="ital">the hide, and sewed it:</hi> (K:) or <hi rend="ital">he measured,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">proportioned,</hi> (<foreign lang="ar">قدّر</foreign>,) <hi rend="ital">the hide,</hi> (JK, S, Msb, K,) <foreign lang="ar">لِمَا يُرِيدُ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">for,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">to, that which he desired</hi> to make of it], (JK, * TA,) or <foreign lang="ar">لِلسِّقَآءِ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">for,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">to, the skin for water or milk</hi> that he desired to make], (Msb,) <hi rend="ital">before cutting it;</hi> (S, K, TA;) <hi rend="ital">he measured it</hi> (<foreign lang="ar">قَاسَهُ</foreign>) <hi rend="ital">to cut from it a water-bag,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">a water-skin,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">a boot:</hi> (TA:) and in like manner, <foreign lang="ar">خَلَقَ النِّطَعَ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">he measured,</hi> &amp;c., <hi rend="ital">the</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">نطع</foreign> [q. v.]: when one cuts it, one says, <foreign lang="ar">فَرَاهُ</foreign>. (K.) And <foreign lang="ar">خَلَقَ النَّعْلَ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">He determined the measure of the sandal,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">proportioned it;</hi> (<foreign lang="ar">قَدَّرَهَا</foreign>;) and <hi rend="ital">made it by measure.</hi> (Ksh and Bd in ii. 19.) Hence the saying of Zuheyr, (S,) praising Herim Ibn-Sinán, (TA,) <pb n="800"/> 
                  <quote>
                     <L>
                        <foreign lang="ar">وَلَأَنْتَ تَفْرِى مَا خَلَقْتَ وَبَعْ</foreign>
                     </L> 
                     <L>
                        <foreign lang="ar">ضُ القَوْمِ يَخْلُقُ ثُمَّ لَا يَفْرِى</foreign>
                     </L> 
                  </quote>
 <note>In the preceding quotation, the final character of the first line and initial character of the second are missing in the original text.</note>[<assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>   <hi rend="ital">And thou indeed cuttest what thou hast measured; but some of the people measure, then will not cut</hi>]: (S, TA:) i. e., when thou determinest upon a thing thou executest it; but others determine upon that which they do not execute. (TA.) And El-Hajjáj said, <foreign lang="ar">مَا خَلَقْتُ إِلَّا قَرَيْتُ وَعَدْتُ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">إِلَّا وَفَيْتُ</foreign> [<assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">I have not measured unless I have</hi> afterwards <hi rend="ital">cut, and I have not promised unless I have</hi> afterwards <hi rend="ital">performed</hi>]. (S.) <foreign lang="ar">أَخْلُقُ لَكُمْ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">مِنَ الطِّينِ كَهَيْئَةِ الطَّيْرِ</foreign>, in the Kur iii. 43, means <hi rend="ital">I will form for you,</hi> (Jel,) or <hi rend="ital">I will make according to its proper measure</hi> (<foreign lang="ar">أُقَدِّرُ</foreign>) <hi rend="ital">for you,</hi> (Ksh, Bd,) and <hi rend="ital">will form,</hi> (Bd,) <hi rend="ital">of clay, a thing like the form of the bird,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">of birds.</hi> (Ksh, Bd, Jel.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  [Hence,] it signifies also The <hi rend="ital">bringing</hi> a thing <hi rend="ital">into existence according to a certain measure,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">proportion, and so as to make it equal</hi> [<hi rend="ital">to another thing</hi>], or <hi rend="ital">uniform</hi> [<hi rend="ital">therewith</hi>]: (Ksh and Bd in ii. 19:) or the <hi rend="ital">originating,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">producing,</hi> [a thing] <hi rend="ital">after a pattern,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">model, which one has devised, not after the similitude of anything preexisting:</hi> this is another meaning which it has in the [classical] language of the Arabs. (TA.) As the act of God, it signifies The <hi rend="ital">originating,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">bringing into being</hi> or <hi rend="ital">existence,</hi> anything, <hi rend="ital">not after the similitude of anything pre-existing:</hi> (TA:) [and the <hi rend="ital">creating</hi> a thing; and thus it is generally best rendered; as meaning the <hi rend="ital">bringing into existence from a state of non-existence:</hi> for] <foreign lang="ar">خَلَقَ ٱللّٰهُ الشَّىْءَ</foreign>, inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">خَلْقٌ</foreign>, means <hi rend="ital">God brought the thing into existence</hi> (Mgh, * TA) <hi rend="ital">after it had not been:</hi> (TA:) [or <foreign lang="ar">خَلْقٌ</foreign>, as the act of God, signifies the <hi rend="ital">creating out of nothing:</hi> for it is said that] <foreign lang="ar">أُعْبُدُوا رَبَّكُمُ ٱلَّذِى خَلَقَكُمْ</foreign>, in the Kur ii. 19, means [<hi rend="ital">Serve ye your Lord</hi>] <hi rend="ital">who brought you into existence when ye were nothing.</hi> (Jel. [But in other passages of the Kur (vi. 2 &amp;c.) it is said that God created (<foreign lang="ar">خَلَقَ</foreign>) mankind of clay.]) Accord. to the A, <foreign lang="ar">خَلَقَ ٱللّٰهُ الخَلْقَ</foreign> is a tropical phrase, meaning <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">God brought into existence the creation,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">created beings,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">mankind, according to a predetermination</hi> (<foreign lang="ar">تَقْدِير</foreign>) <hi rend="ital">required by wisdom.</hi> (TA.) You say, <foreign lang="ar">هٰذِهِ خَلِيقَتُهُ الَّتِى خُلِقَ عَلَيْهَا</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">خُلِقَهَا</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">الَّتِى خُلِقَ</foreign>: see <foreign lang="ar">خُلُقٌ</foreign>. (Lh.)          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  [Hence, also,] <foreign lang="ar">خَلَقَ</foreign>, (S, Msb, K, TA,) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">خَلْقٌ</foreign>, (TA,) <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">He fabricated</hi> speech, or a saying or sentence, &amp;c.: (K, * TA:) <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">he forged</hi> (S, Msb, K, TA) a saying, (Msb,) or a lie, or a falsehood; (S, K, TA;) as also   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n11381-1" target="اختلق" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign> (S, Msb, K) and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n11381-2" target="تخلّق" n="2" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n11381"/></foreign>. (S, K.) The Arabs say, <foreign lang="ar">حَدَّثَنَا</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">فُلَانٌ بِأَحَادِيثِ الخَلْقِ</foreign> <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">Such a one related to us fictitious tales</hi> or <hi rend="ital">stories, such as are deemed pretty,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">such as are told by night</hi> [<hi rend="ital">for entertainment</hi>]. (TA.) And it is said in the Kur [xxvi. 137], accord. to one reading, <foreign lang="ar">إِنْ هٰذَا إِلَّا</foreign>
